======== Scenario: col_necromancer ========
Session Sequence: DaisyAD_Balthazar -> AD_Combat_SendZombie -> AD_ZombieErrandDone
----- Session: DaisyAD_Balthazar -----
Synopsis: On arrival in colony. On encountering Balthazar in room. The necromancer did experiments on the tadpoles here. We know they are magically manipulated. But how?

: The necromancer was experimenting on the tadpoles.
: But they were already imbued with Netherese magic - so where did that magic come from?

----- Session: AD_Combat_SendZombie -----
Synopsis: The necromancer is sending a zombie to light the candles that start an arcane ritual which drains the player's hitpoints and ultimately turns them into a zombie.

Balthazar: Go, light the candles!

Synopsis: This dialog plays upon rolling a passive Arcana check after reading one of the illithid manuscripts in the lower Colony's Memory Library.For tadpoled companions, each companion will see this check once, after reading an illithid manuscript, unless someone else has succeeded this check.For non-tadpoled companions, a different check occurs when they try to read the illithid manuscripts. ======== Scenario: sce_halsin ========
Session Sequence: 
----- Session:  -----
Synopsis: Dialogue with Halsin in the epilogue of Act 2. In it, he reacts to the various states that could occur in relation to his desire to rid the Act 2 region of the shadow curse:- if you've already done everything needed to ensure success. he's grateful and seeks to remain with you on the journey to Baldur's Gate.- if the curse is not yet sure to be lifted, but there's still something that can be done (ie Thaniel was saved from the Shadowfell, but hasn't been fully restored), he will implore the players to help and offer to join them.- if it's no longer possible to lift the curse, Halsin is sad and resigned to staying behind to stand sentry over it. He will not be available as a companion in Act 3, and his story effectively ends here.

Halsin: Thaniel rests still, but it's no easy slumber. || [context] NodeContext: Concerned/Urgent. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Halsin: The shadows rended him in two when they bore him away to the Shadowfell. Half of his essence remained here, amidst the curse. || [context] NodeContext: Concerned/Urgent. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Halsin: What stayed behind would have been the strongest part of him. But after all these years left in darkness, corruption must have taken hold. || [context] NodeContext: Concerned/Urgent. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Player: Tell me how I can help.
Halsin: It's both simple and not - we need to find Thaniel's missing half, and make him whole again. || [context] NodeContext: Concerned/Urgent. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Halsin: Only, the missing half may not come willingly. The curse will have sunk its tendrils deep, twisting Thaniel's essence into something... else. || [context] NodeContext: Some foreboding. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Player: All right, leave it to me. || [approval] ['Astarion -1', 'Gale 1', 'Wyll 1', 'Karlach 1', 'Halsin 10']
Halsin: This doesn't have to be your burden alone. Every moment counts, and I've asked much of you already without being at your side. || [context] NodeContext: Stalwart, heartfelt
Halsin: If you want me, I'm yours. Against the curse, against the Absolute - anything. Just say the word. || [context] NodeContext: Stalwart, heartfelt
Player: Stay here, for now.
Halsin: I'll be ready.

----- Session: Nimble -----

Nimble: Wulbren will get us to the city - I know it. || [context] NodeContext: determined

======== Scenario: sce_minthara ========
Session Sequence: 
----- Session:  -----
Synopsis: After the SCE debrief, Minthara sits on Ketheric's throne and dreams of what lies ahead.

Nightwarden Minthara: You killed the dead man. I'm impressed.
Nightwarden Minthara: And now your path takes you to Baldur's Gate. I shall walk that path with you.
Player: I hoped you would - we make a good team. || [approval] ['Astarion 1', 'Minthara 10']
Player: And I'll never tire of killing their previous occupants. We make a good team. || [approval] ['Astarion 1', 'Minthara 10']
Nightwarden Minthara: We make an acceptable team. But there are greater challenges than Ketheric ahead of us.
Nightwarden Minthara: It is clear, now, that he was not working alone.
[desc] CinematicNodeContext: Leaves throne, standing from here on || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Leaves throne, standing from here on
Nightwarden Minthara: We must be free if we are to rule - and to be free, we must destroy this cult, and Ketheric's co-conspirators along with it.
Nightwarden Minthara: I know one of them all too well - Bhaal's blood-letter, Orin.
Nightwarden Minthara: To think I thought her to be speaking for the Absolute. I worshipped that woman.
Player: So it's personal? Good - let's take her down.
Nightwarden Minthara: You make it sound so simple. She is the Chosen of Bhaal, Lord of Murder, and one of the cult's founders.
Nightwarden Minthara: Indeed, she is the one who indoctrinated me with the Absolute's lies.
Player: There was another with Ketheric - Gortash. Do you know anything about him?
Nightwarden Minthara: Only that he serves Bane, which could make him a petty lordling, or a despot capable of bending the world to his will.
Nightwarden Minthara: That he has enslaved illithids to fulfil his ambitions strongly suggests he is the latter.
Nightwarden Minthara: The Harper may know more - her precious Baldur's Gate was the soil that nourished his growth.

======== Scenario: sce_wulbren ========
Session Sequence: 
----- Session:  -----
Synopsis: This dialogue is peak Wulbren. If he's met you in haven (after you saved him), he rolls back on how rude he was as he realises the player would be an amazing asset in the city. If this is your first time meeting him since the escape (if haven is destroyed he waits out on the river until this scene in the epilogue), he realises how good the player would be to have on his side in the city and tells him all about how wronged the ironhand gnomes were.

Wulbren Bongle: You helped me escape this hellspit, then took down the heart of Moonrise - Ketheric himself. I'm impressed.
Wulbren Bongle: And I'm not a man easily impressed.
Player: I believe the words you're looking for are 'thank you'.
Wulbren Bongle: I was getting to that, but all right - thank you. || [context] NodeContext: a touch annoyed
Wulbren Bongle: Back in my cell, I didn't tell you everything - about who I was, and more importantly, who I represent. || [context] NodeContext: sincere
Wulbren Bongle: I am Wulbren Bongle, leader of the Ironhand Gnomes. No doubt you've heard of us? || [context] NodeContext: said with immense pride
: False
Narrator: *You recall stories of the Ironhand Gnomes - a talented group of inventors who were banished from Baldur's Gate.*
Player: I don't know much, I'm afraid.
Wulbren Bongle: We are inventors of the highest order, matched, perhaps, but never surpassed by the Gondians at the High House of Wonders.
Wulbren Bongle: But our forebears were foolish - complicit with Sarevok's madness over a century past, and so we were banished. Still are to this day.
Player: Pity he never succeeded. || [approval] ['Astarion 1']
Wulbren Bongle: You agree with such machinations? Duly noted.
Wulbren Bongle: I've fought tooth and nail to restore our reputation. Particularly against Gondian detractors who live in glass houses.
Wulbren Bongle: I've filled appeals - pleaded with the High Artificer himself. They've refused us time and again. Now, however, I will make them listen.
Player: Is there anything I can do to help?
Wulbren Bongle: Plenty. Find me in the city, and help us save Baldur's Gate from itself.

======== Scenario: sce_isobelnightsongreunion ========
Session Sequence: 
----- Session:  -----
Synopsis: If Isobel and Nightsong survive Act 2 they will be having a heartfelt reunion during the Epilogue

Nightsong: Ho! But we have met. This is the soldier that freed me most valiantly from the Shadowfell.
Nightsong: They watched my boot crush the very brain of villainy - and fought well against your changèd father. || [context] NodeContext: old timey change-ed
Isobel: May he rest in peace at last, now that he's dead. || [context] NodeContext: About her father. Tinged with sadness but not too sad. She's about to thank the player warmly.
Isobel: I have more to thank you for than I knew. And we have much to discuss. Perhaps we could join you in your camp later?
Player: Firstly, allow me to apologise to Dame Aylin. My actions were strategy - not personal. || [approval] ['Karlach 1', 'Gale 1', 'Wyll 1', 'Astarion 1', 'Shadowheart 1', "Lae'zel 1", 'Minthara 1']
Nightsong: My forgiveness will be the same. I'd be a fool to turn down a powerful ally - especially one who has earned the trust of fair Isobel.
Nightsong: But Dame Aylin's life is neverending. And she does not forget. Now - I believe Isobel asked a question of you. We will meet you in your camp - is it agreed?
Player: It's a little crowded already.
Isobel: We'll make our visit brief. Cleric's honour.
Player: Fine. I'll see you at camp.
Isobel: Very good. We look forward to it.
Nightsong: Now - you will leave us. We must take succour in one another's bodies and words.
Isobel: Aylin. We'll see you later. || [context] NodeContext: Hushing Aylin for saying something embarassing, but good-natured

======== Scenario: hav_takingisobel ========
Session Sequence: JaheiraCallToArm -> PAD_SpyTransformationClue -> IsobelSaved -> AD_SpyAtEntrance -> AD_FollowUp -> AD_ReactingToRoofNoise -> FollowUpSaved
----- Session: JaheiraCallToArm -----
Synopsis: Isobel is being attacked. Jaheira calls people to defend Isobel, as their lives depend on her.This dialog can happen anywhere in Last Light, but mainly close to Isobel's room.

Jaheira: To arms! Protect Isobel at all cost! || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Focus should be on the shoulders up to obscure whether or not Jaheira has a weapon in hand (cannot be guaranteed).NodeContext: Shouted during the onset of battle

----- Session: PAD_SpyTransformationClue -----
Synopsis: If we go up on the roof above Isobel’s room, we’ll find discarded FF armour and some bloodstains from a transformation of some kind. A successful med check shows someone burst out of their armour (Marcus)

Player: Someone - something - shed Flaming Fist armour like a second skin.

----- Session: IsobelSaved -----
Synopsis: Once the Flaming Fist has been defeated, a shaken Isobel urges players who helped her to go and assist with the fight in the main room. She is coughing and unwell.

Isobel: Help the others - hurry! || [context] NodeContext: Doubled over coughing but telling player not to worry about her.

----- Session: AD_SpyAtEntrance -----
Synopsis: Fallback AD for the flaming fist spy. If he didn't vouch for the player in Entering Haven, he sticks around after the scene, this is to give the chance to the player to notice him. As soon as the player approaches him though, he starts walking away. The player shouldn't normally be able to click on him before he starts moving, but I can't garantee that some frame delay might happen... So this is a vary short AD, a feedback in case the player manages to click on him. He'll say it while turning around and moving away. The player can later talk to him in the dialog HAV_TakingIsobel_FlamingSpy.

Fist Marcus: Need to be back at my post.

----- Session: AD_FollowUp -----
Synopsis: |After the ghoul attack (aka inn attack) Jaheira does this AD to catch the player's attention, while walking to them to talk to them. Player is in there not to speak but to allow tag and flag checks|

Jaheira: You! What happened?

----- Session: AD_ReactingToRoofNoise -----
Synopsis: The player is walking on the roof above Isobel's room and VoiceBarking about the Flaming Spy's transformation leftovers. Isobel reacts if she is close enough to hear.

Isobel: Who's stomping around up there?

----- Session: FollowUpSaved -----
Synopsis: Jaheira and Isobel (and the player) reunite after the fight with Marcus. Jaheira is relieved Isobel hasn't been captured. Isobel debriefs with player and sends them off on their main mission for Act 2. Both of them will be in heightened mood, having just survived a fierce battle- not totally out of breath, but still recovering from the immediate battle.

Jaheira: Isobel! Are you all right? || [context] InternalNodeContext: To IsobelNodeContext: Relieved. If Isobel had been taken, things would be very bad
Isobel: I'm fine. || [context] NodeContext: Reassuring - Isobel's survival means the survival of the entire region, so she's saying 'I'm all good, let's worry about more important things'
Jaheira: Marcus has been with us since the start - they've been tracking us this whole time. || [context] InternalNodeContext: To Isobel
Jaheira: And that was no random attack - you were the target, Isobel. They know how important you are. || [context] InternalNodeContext: To Isobel
Jaheira: But they don't know about you. || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Addressed to playerInternalNodeContext: To player
Jaheira: Isobel - this is -
Isobel: The True Soul who saved my life.

======== Scenario: hav_jaheira ========
Session Sequence: MeetsHalsin -> AD_AtCheckpoint -> AD_PlayersAttackJaheira
----- Session: MeetsHalsin -----
Synopsis: Halsin and Jaheira conversation to catch them not being a true soul like she's looking for. Instead they have a civil conversation, but bearly do more than scratch the surface

Jaheira: The Archdruid Halsin. Do not be surprised that I know your name - you fit a rather singular description.
Jaheira: And one survivor of the shadow curse's fall ought to know another.
Player: No one who witnessed that battle is likely to forget it.
Jaheira: Not the battle, nor what came after.
Jaheira: Those of us who saw the birth of the shadow curse seem doomed to return, and bear witness to its work again.
Jaheira: But I ought to warn you, Halsin. Much as it shames me - it is not the curse I come to cleanse, but the cult.
Player: You don't have to explain yourself to me.
Jaheira: Don't I? We both left this land with a half-victory in hand at most - but only one of us settled for it.
Jaheira: It has become my way, perhaps, to always have one eye on the next fight. For better or worse, that is the cult.
Jaheira: Though I will not be the one to fight it, I think. The one you journey with - we have already spoken of infiltrating Moonrise.
Jaheira: One carrying a tadpole - a True Soul - might be able to reach Ketheric. And then... perhaps we will find a way to fight both our battles.

He doesn't feel like a hero though - he feels like a failure.

======== Scenario: moo_dridercaravan ========
Session Sequence: AD_GoingForBreak
----- Session: AD_GoingForBreak -----
Synopsis: |Goblins just finished their escort job with the drider caravan. They deserve some rest.|

Sharp-Eye Lora: Ah. You survived this run. || [context] NodeContext: Just finished a dangerous patrol - spoken to a friend as if pleasantly surprised (a joke)
Warrior Gronag: You and all. || [context] NodeContext: Responding as if pleasantly surprised his friend survived.
Sharp-Eye Lora: Drink? || [context] NodeContext: Raised eyebrow to friend - this is what they always do
Warrior Gronag: Drink. || [context] NodeContext: A confirmation in response to "Drink?" from a friend.

======== Scenario: moo_bazaar ========
Session Sequence: PAD_SharranObservation -> Zhent02 -> AD_BugbearThrow -> BazaarStander_006 -> BazaarStander_007 -> Guard01 -> Bystander01 -> Bystander00 -> Guard00 -> AD_GoblinsListening -> AD_BazEntranceGuard_002 -> Bystander02 -> Zhent00 -> AD_ZhentarimCrew -> BazaarStander_005 -> Zhent01 -> Bystander04 -> BazEntranceGuard

Synopsis: A Zhentarim agent guarding Roah Moonglow. She's looking around at the growing power of the church and feeling wary of it.

Yerle: Ain't looking to convert, True Soul. Gods mind their mess, I mind mine. || [context] NodeContext: Respectful but flat refusal - most Absolutists want to convert others, and she's pre-empting it.

----- Session: BazaarStander_006 -----
Synopsis: A novice of the church of the Absolute, by turns praying to herself or speaking to us, who she sees as a leading follower of her god

Pilgrim Nalira: The prisoners below are gone, True Soul. I cannot understand why they would flee Her mercy. || [context] InternalNodeContext: The prisoners successfully escaped from Moonrise's dungeons (perhaps all, perhaps only one)NodeContext: Confused, hurt - prisoners in the cell escaped - she saw them as heathens her church was trying to 'save'

----- Session: BazaarStander_007 -----
Synopsis: This novice has joined the church in the hopes of being elevated to True Soul. She's not here for personal gain, but seeking an actual religious experience - one she believes we've already been blessed to have.

You will return changed, I'm sure of it. || [context] InternalNodeContext: The player has kidnapped Isobel and helped return Nightsong and Balthazar to Moonrise. The army of the Absolute is ready to march.NodeContext: Wishing us well - we're about to get our 'reward'

----- Session: Guard01 -----
Synopsis: A guard watching the alarm system on the ground floor of Moonrise Tower. He love and respects authority, and enjoys the thought of failure being punished.

Adept Furek: You should go through the main hall. Witnessing the General's justice is an honour.

----- Session: Bystander01 -----
Synopsis: A goblin on the floor of Moonrise Towers, chatting absently while being a bystander. His commentary changes depending on how the player handled the grove.

Brawler Weneg: Heard a rumour some do-gooder stopped a horde of Absolutists from getting their hands on a load of druids in some grove.
Brawler Weneg: Whoever it was better pray the General doesn't smoke 'em out. Be a bloodbath, so it would.

----- Session: Bystander00 -----
Synopsis: A goblin on the floor of Moonrise Towers, chatting absently while being a bystander. This one is worried about the other goblins that were sent to the execution room.

Brawler Orik: You're the best True Soul I ever met.

----- Session: Guard00 -----
Synopsis: A guard watching the alarm system on the ground floor of Moonrise Tower. He's brusque to anyone who approaches.

Adept Dorikel: I saw it, True Soul. The army. They're nearly ready. It's nearly time.
Player: Which army do you mean?
Adept Dorikel: Us. We are so many. And we are marching to Baldur's Gate, as soon as the Absolute gives word.
Adept Dorikel: I've never been to battle. I've never been to war. But I feel so... calm. Ready.

----- Session: AD_GoblinsListening -----
Synopsis: The Bazaar Goblins are listening into the execution, worried about their own necks.

Brawler Weneg: Enough! Just leave the bloody True Souls to their business.
Brawler Wim: And what's to say that couldn't be us? They say the General rewards them as serve him well.
Brawler Orik: And what about them who hang around his door like a bad smell?

----- Session: AD_BazEntranceGuard_002 -----
Synopsis: The guard points the player towards the execution room after they first enter the tower.

Zealot Brinn: Another True Soul. The Disciple will want to see you - through the main doors.

----- Session: Bystander02 -----
Synopsis: A goblin on the floor of Moonrise Towers, chatting absently while being a bystander.

Brawler Wim: We ought to head out now - burn everything between here and the city.

----- Session: Zhent00 -----
Synopsis: A Zhentarim trader from the goblin camp. Roah will react based on your actions if you've met her, or give a brief summary of the Zhentarim's connection to the Absolute if not.

Roah Moonglow: Ah, a new face come to bask in the light of the Absolute. How can I be of service, True Soul?
Player: Are you a follower of the Absolute?
Roah Moonglow: Blessed by association, let's say. I come to pay proper respect to a new power.
Roah Moonglow: I'd bow, but the Zhentarim prefer to look their business partners in the eye.
Player: 'The Zhentarim'?
Roah Moonglow: Merchants like any other. Though we tend to see opportunity where others don't.

----- Session: AD_ZhentarimCrew -----
Synopsis: Inside Moonrise Towers, the Zhentarim Guards and Merchant are making a deal with a rising cult. These are their idle exchanges.

Roah Moonglow: Smile, Yerle. We're among friends. || [context] NodeContext: Half-mocking, half-prodding. Her dour bodyguards are looking around at cultists suspiciously
Yerle: Too damn friendly, you ask me. Gods-fearing folk ought to be more... fearful. || [context] NodeContext: The cultists bother her - they're too friendly, too faithful. It's not right.
Roah Moonglow: Why not join this Absolute, see what all the fuss is about? || [context] NodeContext: Smirking
Yerle: ...I'll stick with the monster I know, thanks. || [context] NodeContext: Wry, knows she's being mocked  - she's referring to her boss, who she knows is tougher than any cultist of the Absolute

----- Session: BazaarStander_005 -----
Synopsis: A supplicant who has just arrived at the seat of his religion. He  survived a harrowing journey through cursed lands - his family did not, and he is trying to rationalise that, becoming all the more fanaticin the process.

Pilgrim Farimorn: Blessings, True Soul. We're to march soon - thanks to you. || [context] InternalNodeContext: The player has kidnapped Isobel and helped return Nightsong and Balthazar to Moonrise. The army of the Absolute is ready to march.NodeContext: Awed by you

----- Session: Zhent01 -----
Synopsis: A Zhentarim agent guarding a trader from her organisation.

Erna: You trying to get me in trouble? || [context] NodeContext: Smiling but fobbing us off.

----- Session: Bystander04 -----
Synopsis: This human is waiting to speak to Z'rell. A big tough guy but is full  of hope that the Absolute will be proud of him. Should have a faint air of a stalker.

Pilgrim Iong: The Disciple has returned upstairs but... perhaps she'll still see me. || [context] NodeContext: Wants to go, psyching himself up a bit. Now he has his chance and he's a bit scared

----- Session: BazEntranceGuard -----
Synopsis: Standing at the entrance of Moonrise Tower, the guard is keeping eye on all the fresh blood seeking audience with the Absolute. The player can influence the guard to send the pilgrims to their death in Town, or to take a chance on them and send them as fodder to colony. Either way the pilgrims will have a bad time.

Acolyte Belub: Each pack of 'recruits' they bring in is worse than the last. || [context] InternalNodeContext: Belub is not impressed by the new pilgrims who have shown up to join the Absolutes cause.
Acolyte Belub: Can't trust them to sweep the stables, let alone swing a sword.
Player: Then get rid of them. The undeserving should be purged.
Acolyte Belub: I-  yeah. Yeah, they're dead weight. Not real believers like us. || [context] NodeContext: Slowly coming around to an opinion

======== Scenario: moo_audience ========

----- Session: Ketheric -----
Synopsis: Evil route. Captured Nightsong

Ketheric Thorm: I'll tell you a story, True Soul. About a man who sold himself piece by piece.
Ketheric Thorm: He had... everything. A wonderful wife. A brilliant daughter. They lived not far from here.
Ketheric Thorm: His wife died too young. Grief tore through their home like a thief, snatching away the scent of her hair, the rustle of her skirts. But the man did not break.
Ketheric Thorm: He could not break. His daughter needed him whole, after all.
Ketheric Thorm: She grew up - grew strong. Challenged him. Filled his heart with such joy it supplanted all sorrow.
Ketheric Thorm: When she was killed, the man... he tried to remain whole, but it wasn't possible. Do you understand?

Ketheric Thorm: The pain was unbearable. All-consuming. He decided he'd do anything for reprieve.
Ketheric Thorm: First, he sold himself to the goddess of loss. But the pain did not subside, no matter his obscene feats of devotion.
Ketheric Thorm: Then a new god came - a god who promised the man something wonderful: his daughter. Her life returned. Imagine it.
Ketheric Thorm: He would have to give everything: his body and soul entire. He did not hesitate. Not for a moment.
Ketheric Thorm: And the new god did as promised. The man's brilliant, beautiful daughter came back. She was whole - she was alive. But she despised the pitiful wretch her father had become.
Ketheric Thorm: Her hatred he could bear, perhaps, as long as she had another chance to live.
Ketheric Thorm: Everything I've done, everything I have built, has been to give Isobel that chance. And you, True Soul - you have squandered it.
Player: You brought her back once. Do it again.
Ketheric Thorm: I can. I will. But it is not without cost. Who will pay this time, True Soul?

======== Scenario: sha_crypt ========
Session Sequence: PAD_PuzzlePlaque -> AD_CandlestickCountdown -> PAD_StatueReaction -> AD_MagicSkull
----- Session: PAD_PuzzlePlaque -----
Synopsis: PAD used for when players interact with the plaque at the entrance of the crypt. Read by the narrator as an object AD.

Narrator: *The answer lies in darkness.*

----- Session: AD_CandlestickCountdown -----
Synopsis: 

Umbral Gem: |3...|
Umbral Gem: |2...|
Umbral Gem: |1...|
Umbral Gem: |0|

----- Session: PAD_StatueReaction -----
Synopsis: Players enter the crypt and react to the statue.

Player: | That's a big statue. |

----- Session: AD_MagicSkull -----
Synopsis: The skull taunts the player to not go forward, declaring that everything is already being handled.

Herald of Balthazar: Not wanted. Not needed. Leave. || [context] NodeContext: Ill-tempered warning from a skull being remotely voiced by a necromancer.

======== Scenario: sha_disc ========
Session Sequence: PAD_Unlocked -> Altar
----- Session: PAD_Unlocked -----
Synopsis: Players unlock the disc/platform in the Shar temple for the first time.

Player: The disc is moving. This must lead to the next part of Shar's Gauntlet. || [context] InternalNodeContext: This node if you received knowledge of the Shar trials from the disc altar.NodeContext: [Astarion: 'bloody' as in annoying, not 'lots of blood]

Synopsis: The player approaches an altar dedicated to Shar. This altar is a call to action for the player to complete Shar's trials and become a Dark Justiciar.

Narrator: *The inscription's challenge remains the same.*
Shadowheart: There's nothing more for us to do here - not until we complete Lady Shar's trials.

======== Scenario: sha_mausoleum ========
Session Sequence: PAD_MyrkulSymbol -> PAD_MakeshiftVessel -> PAD_KethericsMap -> PAD_FoundIsobelsPlaque -> PAD_SkullBalthazaarIntro -> PAD_FoundDisc -> PAD_NecromancersRoom -> PAD_DisarmedPressurePlate -> PAD_KethericsWifePlaque
----- Session: PAD_MyrkulSymbol -----
Synopsis: Players enter the room where the symbol of Myrkul lies on the floor. Hard religion DC before the PAD plays.

Player: What is that symbol supposed to mean?

----- Session: PAD_MakeshiftVessel -----
Synopsis: Players find a vessel with a half-formed humanoid shape gestating inside and reacts accordingly. The being is just inert flesh and cannot speak.

Player: What is that? Almost looks like someone was trying to grow a person.

----- Session: PAD_KethericsMap -----
Synopsis: Players find the map Ketheric had inside the mausoleum. It shows  the entrance to the Shar Temple (behind Isobel's tomb) and has notes on an attack.

Player: Looks like there's a temple under this place - and something deadly sealed inside it.

----- Session: PAD_FoundIsobelsPlaque -----
Synopsis: PAD for characters reacting to finding Isobels plaque in the Ketheric Mausoleum. Has 3 reaction states:- Already know Ketheric is Isobel's Father- Don't know aboutfamily relationship but have met Isobel- Don't know about family relationship and haven't met Isobel

Player: Isobel. That's the name of the cleric at Last Light Inn, right?
Player: Can she possibly be Ketheric's daughter?

----- Session: PAD_SkullBalthazaarIntro -----
Synopsis: Party reacts to a magic-mouth skull that projects Balthazar's voice, warning them to leave.

Player: Balthazar, a necromancer lap dog of Ketheric Thorm's.
Player: Who knows what he may have up his rotten sleeve.
Player: We need to stay alert.

----- Session: PAD_FoundDisc -----
Synopsis: Players find the disc at the mausoleum that leads to the Shar temple.

Player: That disc looks like it can move - but where does it lead? || [context] NodeContext: SH - surprise/awe.

----- Session: PAD_NecromancersRoom -----
Synopsis: Players enter for the first time inside the necromancer's room at the mausoleum. Bones are scattered about and arranged into strange totems, in a sign someone has been dabbling in dark magic.

Player: Bones everywhere... Someone's been engaging in dark rituals here. || [context] NodeContext: Astarion; as in 'water water everywhere, but not a drop to drink' (referring to a large amount of skeletons on display in a tomb

----- Session: PAD_DisarmedPressurePlate -----
Synopsis: Player steps with a pressure plate that should trigger the trap in the mausoleum but nothing happens.

Player: Nothing - it must have been disarmed. || [context] NodeContext: Stepped on a trap, but nothing happened

----- Session: PAD_KethericsWifePlaque -----
Synopsis: Reaction from player/narrator who interacts with the tomb of Isobel's mother (and Ketheric's wife).

Narrator: *Here lies Melodia Thorm, beloved wife and mother. Ai armiel telere maenen hir.* || [context] NodeContext: Ah-less-ia /  Ay Army-el Teller-eh Man-en here

======== Scenario: sha_orthon ========
Session Sequence: PAD_VictimsDisplay -> AD_FormLines -> AD_MineClusterAbility -> AD -> AD_TransitionsToSecondPhase
----- Session: PAD_VictimsDisplay -----
Synopsis: In Shar temple, there is a number of mutilated corpses - justiciars killed by Orthon. But he not only killed them, but he also created various installments of them, put them on spikes, hang them, etc

Player: A very gory idea of art.

----- Session: AD_FormLines -----
Synopsis: Orthon tells the merregons to get close to him during combat.

Yurgir: Form up ranks! Don't let anything get past you! || [context] NodeContext: During combat. Bellowing orders to his merregon soldiers to change formation

----- Session: AD_MineClusterAbility -----
Synopsis: Spoken as the orthon throws timed explosives at the player during combat.

======== Scenario: twn_finale ========
Session Sequence: LeavingAct
----- Session: LeavingAct -----
Synopsis: Scene of players leaving SCL to travel to Intermezzo. This scene triggers when the party leave Moonrise Tower after defeating Ketheric. There are two variants. One where the curse has been lifted, one where the curse hasn't been lifted.If the curse has been lifted, Halsin and/or Art Cullagh will be present at Moonrise if alive, and will tell players that the quest has succeeded, and that when they leave Moonrise, they'll see the restults. They tell you to wrap up your business here first. This happens in the dialogues for those characters, not here.If the curse hasn't been lifted, players see a vista of the shadow-cursed lands on leaving Moonrise, and move on toward the Risen Road.

Narrator: *The curse has been lifted, the lands cleansed of the shadows. Ketheric's reign of living death is over.* || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Players leave SCL by the Risen Road. They look back to see beams of light breaking through the clouds.-The curse has been lifted. The clouds above part, and a powerful beam of moonlight shines through and illuminates the town centre where the statue of Ketheric stood. It is now shattered.
Narrator: *Your courage has been tested, and in this, at least, you have triumphed.* || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Cut to close up of the shattered statue. An enormous silver tree bursts through the ground where the statue once stood, silver leaves/fruits sprouting, and the light from above intensifies as the shadows disperse.
[desc] CinematicNodeContext: Cut back to party, with Halsin in shot, looking across the rejuvenating region. Halsin takes front and centre, looking back across the 'healed'vista, overjoyed, and then the party turn and continue their journey || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Cut back to party, with Halsin in shot, looking across the rejuvenating region. Halsin takes front and centre, looking back across the 'healed'vista, overjoyed, and then the party turn and continue their journey

Session Sequence: Brewer_Zombie_01 -> ResearchNotes -> AD_Brewer_Zombie_02 -> AD_Brewer_Zombie_03 -> AD_Brewer_Hallucinating_001_Combat -> AD_HalflingsSign -> PAD_Entrance_1P -> AD_Brewer -> AD_WaningMoonSign -> AD_Brewer_Zombie_04 -> AD_Brewer_Necro_Combat -> AD_Brewer_Physical_Combat -> AD_Brewer_Drunk_003_Combat -> PAD_Brewer_CombatStarted -> AD_Brewer_Poison_Combat -> PAD_Brewer_Hallucinating -> PAD_BrewerDead -> Brewer_Zombie_04 -> AD_Brewer_Lightning_Combat -> Brewer -> AD_Brewer_Drunk_002_Combat -> AD_Brewer_Zombie_01 -> Brewer_Zombie_02 -> PAD_Brewer_PassedOut

----- Session: ResearchNotes -----
Synopsis: Research notes of the Brewer.He experimented with different poisons on different creatures, trying to figure out the most effective ways of poisoning them. This book also contains info about his attempts to create a Purple Worm Poison.

Narrator: *Research notes. They describe a powerful venom extracted from a rare purple worm. Distiller Thisobald Thorm sought to create a fatal poison using the worm's gullet.*
Narrator: *He procured several parts of a gullet, but rinsed one in error. The poison he brewed was noxious - but not fatal.*
Narrator: *He devoted months to formulating a deadly poison with the remaining ingredients, without success.*
Narrator: *After exhaustive experimentation, he was able to make a near-deadly extract from the glands. But to complete his poison, Thisobald required one last ingredient:*
Narrator: *The petals of a corpse rose.*
Narrator: *The book's index reveals corpse roses may grow near tombs, mausoleums, and particularly redolent cadavers.*
Narrator: *Thisobald enlisted a courier from Baldur's Gate to obtain corpse rose petals and other ingredients and deliver them to a covert location.*
Narrator: *Unfortunately, a deep purple stain darkens the final page, obscuring the parcel's destination.*
Player: Focus your eyes on the page. Mentally separate the blank ink from the purple stain.
: False
Narrator: *The page is a mess of dark colour. The delivery's location remains a mystery.*

----- Session: Brewer -----
